var fsRenderDate = null;
try {
    var inStorage = localStorage.getItem('__fullscreen_render_data__') || 'null';
    fsRenderDate = JSON.parse(inStorage);
} catch (e) {}

if (fsRenderDate && fsRenderDate.timestamp + 10800000 < Date.now()) {
    fsRenderDate = null
}

var renderFullscreen =
    true && (
    !fsRenderDate
    || 1 === null
    || (1 !== null && fsRenderDate.count < 1
     && fsRenderDate.lastRenderTimestamp + 0 < Date.now())
    || window.location.href.indexOf('showFullscreen=1') > -1
);

function rollbackFullscreenDataHandler (e) {
    if (!e.detail || !e.detail.isInlineFullscreenSkipped) {
        return;
    }

    localStorage.setItem(
        '__fullscreen_render_data__',
        JSON.stringify(fsRenderDate)
    );
}

const onFsReady = (isStub) => () => {
    const isEmpty = isStub || window.__isInlineFullscreenSkipped;
    window.__fullscreenRenderEnded = { isEmpty };
    window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('fullscreenRenderEnded', {
        detail: { isEmpty }
    }));

    if (isEmpty) {
        return;
    }

    var item = {
        timestamp: fsRenderDate ? fsRenderDate.timestamp : Date.now(),
        lastRenderTimestamp: Date.now(),
        count: fsRenderDate ? fsRenderDate.count + 1 : 1
    }
    localStorage.setItem(
        '__fullscreen_render_data__',
        JSON.stringify(item)
    );

    window.removeEventListener('mobileBranding', rollbackFullscreenDataHandler);
    window.addEventListener('mobileBranding', rollbackFullscreenDataHandler);
}

window.hsmCreativeManagerReady.then((m) => m.on('slotCreated', (slot) => {
    if (!slot || slot.adunit !== 'fullscreen') {
        return;
    }

    const type = '';
    const fullscreenBannerBlacklist = 
        '';

    if (false && type){
        slot.config.type = type;
    }

    if (fullscreenBannerBlacklist) {
        slot.config.fullscreenBannerBlacklist = fullscreenBannerBlacklist.split(',');
    }

    if (!renderFullscreen) {
        slot.destroy();
    }

    slot.once('stub', onFsReady(true));
    slot.once('display', onFsReady(false));
}));


    function clearPodlojka () {
        document.querySelectorAll("a.branding").forEach(el => el.remove());
    }

    window.hsmCreativeManagerReady.then((manager) => {
        manager.on('slotCreated', (slot) => {
            if (!slot) {
                return;
            }

            if (slot.adunit === 'podlojka') {
                slot.on('beforeRefresh', clearPodlojka);
                slot.on('beforeDestroy', clearPodlojka);
            }
        });

        manager.ready.then(() => {

    console.log('branding has been rendered');
    var branding = document.createElement('a');
    document.querySelector('#app .app').classList.add(
        'app_branding',
        options.isTypeParallel ? 'app_parallel-branding' : 'app_p-branding'
    );
    document.getElementById('podlojka').parentNode.appendChild(branding);
    var isHTML = options.backgroundType === 'HTML';
    var backgroundImage = isHTML ? '' : 'url(' + options.backgroundImage + ')';
    branding.style.background = [
        options.backgroundColor,
        backgroundImage,
        options.backgroundPosition,
        options.backgroundRepeat,
        options.backgroundAttachment
    ].join(' ');
    branding.classList.add('branding');

    if (isHTML) {
        var iframe = document.createElement('iframe');
        iframe.src = options.backgroundImage;
        iframe.setAttribute('style', 'width:100%;height:100%;border:none;');
        branding.appendChild(iframe);

        if (options.link) {
            var overlay = document.createElement('div');
            overlay.setAttribute('style', 'width:100%;height:100%;top:0;left:0;position:absolute;z-index:1;');
            branding.appendChild(overlay);
        }
    }

    if (options.link) {
        branding.href = options.link;
        branding.target = options.target;
    }

    window.__brandingType = options.isTypeParallel
        ? 'II'
        : 'П';
    window.__isExclusiveBranding = /total/.test(options.isExclusive);
    window.__isTotalExclusiveBranding = options.isExclusive === 'total_infinity_scroll';
    window.__shouldHideFlyroll = options.shouldHideFlyroll;
    window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('setBrandingType', {
        detail: {
            brandingType: window.__brandingType,
            isExclusiveBranding: window.__isExclusiveBranding,
            isTotalExclusiveBranding: window.__isTotalExclusiveBranding,
            shouldHideFlyroll: window.__shouldHideFlyroll
        }
    }));

    if (window.__isTotalExclusiveBranding) {
        window.removeEventListener('blur', onBlur);
        window.removeEventListener('focus', onFocus);
        clearTimeout(timeout);
    }
}


window.setHbTopSticky = function (options) {
    window.__isHbTopSticky = options.isHbTopSticky;
    window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('stickyHbTop', {
        detail: {
            isHbTopSticky: options.isHbTopSticky
        }
    }));
}


window.renderStubBanner = function (options) {
    window.__inImageBannerType = options.inImageBannerType;
    window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('inImageBannerType', {
        detail: {
            inImageBannerType: options.inImageBannerType
        }
    }));
}


window.inreadRenderParams = function (options) {
    window.__isInreadFlyRoll = options.isInreadFlyRoll;
    window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('inreadFlyRoll', {
        detail: {
            isInreadFlyRoll: options.isInreadFlyRoll
        }
    }));
}

        detail: {
            isVb1Exclusive: options.isVb1Exclusive
        }
    }));
}
